  312  ************************************************************************
  313  *     Anzeige der Materialbestände in einem Zeitintervall              *
  314  ************************************************************************
  315  *  Der Report gliedert sich im wesentlichen in folgende Verarbeitungs- *
  316  *  blöcke:                                                             *
  317  *  1) Definition des Einstiegsbildes und Vorbelegung einzelner         *
  318  *     Selektionsfelder, sowie Prüfung der eingegebenen Selektions-     *
  319  *     parameter und Berechtigungsprüfung                               *
  320  *  2) Lesen der aktuellen Bestandswerte                                *
  321  *  3) Lesen und Verarbeiten der Materialbelege                         *
  322  *  4) Berechnung der Bestandswerte zu den vorgegebenen Datümern        *
  323  *  5) Ausgabe der Bestände und Materialbelege                          *
  324  ************************************************************************

 3076
 3077  *  Aus dieser Unterroutine heraus werden implizit, d.h. in der Schleife
 3078  *  über alle selektierten Bestände, die zugehörigen Materialbelege
 3079  *  aufgerufen.
 3080  *  Die Bestände werden zum Anfangs- und Enddatum als Summen zu
 3081  *  folgendem Schlüssel, der im Listkopf geführt wird, ausgegeben:
 3082  *  Buchungskreis bzw. Werk, Material, Charge. Nicht-chargenpflichtige
 3083  *  Materialien werden auf Materialebene angezeigt.
 3084  *  Es folgt jeweils eine Liste mit den einzelnen Belegpositionen.
 3085
 3086  *********************** Ende HAUPTPROGRAMM *****************************
 3087  *
 3088  ************************* FORMROUTINEN *********************************
 3089
 3090  *&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
 3091  *&      Form  EINGABEN_PRUEFEN
 3092  *&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
 3093  *       Prüfung der Eingaben auf dem Selektionsbild                    *
 3094  *----------------------------------------------------------------------*
 3095  FORM eingaben_pruefen.
 3096
 3097  * check the entries only in releases >= 46B
 3098    CALL FUNCTION 'MMIM_ENTRYCHECK_MAIN'
 3099      TABLES
 3100        it_matnr = matnr
 3101        it_werks = werks
 3102        it_lgort = lgort
 3103        it_bwart = bwart
 3104        it_bukrs = bukrs.
 3105
 3106  *  Die Selektionseingaben Buchungskreis und Werk werden hierarchisch
 3107  *  verstanden, d.h. es werden nur Werke innerhalb der angegebenen
 3108  *  Buchungskreise selektiert.
 3109  *  Lagerort-/Chargenbestand: Da die Werksbezeichnung eindeutig ist,
 3110  *  finden alle Selektionen auf Werksebene bzw. - falls mindestens ein
 3111  *  Lagerort eingegeben wurde - auf der Ebene der eingegebenen Lagerorte
 3112  *  statt. Die Ausgabe erfolgt auf Werksebene des Materials / der Charge.
 3113  *  Bewerteter Bestand: Die Ausgabe erfolgt auf Bewertungskreisebene,
 3114  *  d.h. je nach Einstellung in der Tabelle TCURM auf Werks- oder
 3115  *  Buchungskreisebene.
 3116
 3117  *  Feststellen, ob der Bewertungskreis auf Buchungskreis- oder
 3118  *  Werksebene liegt:
 3119  *  tcurm-bwkrs_cus = 1  =>  Bewertungskreis auf Werksebene,
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
21.07.26 S2A      Program RM07MLBD                              Page     54
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 3120  *  tcurm-bwkrs_cus = 3  =>  Bewertungskreis auf Buchungskreisebene.
 3121    SELECT bwkrs_cus FROM tcurm INTO curm
 3122              ORDER BY PRIMARY KEY.
 3123    ENDSELECT.
 3124
 3125    IF xchar = ' ' AND NOT charg-low IS INITIAL.
 3126      xchar = 'X'.
 3127    ENDIF.

 3129      xchar = 'X'.
 3130    ENDIF.                                                    "838360_^

 3132    IF sbbst = 'X' AND sobkz IS INITIAL.
 3133      MESSAGE e286.
 3134  *   Bitte ein Sonderbestandskennzeichen eingeben.
 3135    ELSEIF sbbst = ' ' AND NOT sobkz IS INITIAL.
 3136      CLEAR sobkz.
 3137      MESSAGE w287.
 3138  *   Sonderbestandskennzeichen wird zurückgesetzt.
 3139    ENDIF.
 3140
 3141  * reset the entries for plant when valuation area is        "n599218
 3142  * company code and mode is valuated stock                   "n599218
 3143    IF     curm  = '3'      AND                               "n599218
 3144           bwbst = 'X'.                                       "n599218
 3145      IF  NOT werks[]  IS INITIAL.                            "n599218
 3146  *     reset the restricts for plants                        "n599218
 3147        CLEAR                  werks.                         "n599218
 3148        REFRESH                werks.                         "n599218
 3149  *     text-074 : valuation area = company code              "n599218
 3150  *     text-075 : entries for plant will be reset            "n599218

 3152      ENDIF.                                                  "n599218
 3153    ENDIF.                                                    "n599218

 3156      OR bwbst = 'X' AND NOT xchar IS INITIAL.

 3159  *   Charge wird zurückgesetzt.
 3160    ENDIF.
 3161    IF bwbst = 'X' AND NOT lgort IS INITIAL.
 3162      CLEAR lgort. REFRESH lgort.
 3163      MESSAGE w284.
 3164  *   Lagerort wird zurückgesetzt.
 3165    ENDIF.

 3168  * special stock indicator

 3170    CLEAR                      g_ra_sobkz.

 3172    IF      lgbst = 'X'.       "only Storage loc./batch stock
 3173  *   create ranges table : select only sobkz = space
 3174      PERFORM f0500_append_ra_sobkz   USING  c_space.
 3175
 3176    ELSEIF  bwbst = 'X'.       "only valuated stocks
 3177  *   take all special stock indicators / the record selection
 3178  *   will be done after the database selection
 3179
 3180    ELSEIF  sbbst = 'X'.       "only special stocks
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
21.07.26 S2A      Program RM07MLBD                              Page     55
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 3181      PERFORM f0500_append_ra_sobkz   USING  sobkz.
 3182

 3184
 3185  "{ Begin ENHO DIPCS_RM07MLBD001 IS-AD-SSP AD_SUB }
 3186  * DI A&D SSP

 3638  *&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
 3639  *&      Form  SUMMEN_BILDEN
 3640  *&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
 3641  *       Bestandssummen zur Berechnung der Bestände                     *
 3642  *       zu 'datum-low' und 'datum-high'                                *
 3643  *----------------------------------------------------------------------*
 3644  FORM summen_bilden.
 3645  * Some explanatory words on the strategy of material
 3646  * counting/valuation:
 3647  * ======================================================
 3648  * 1) Stock overview (no valuation):
 3649  *    The material document is accepted, if is has not been created
 3650  *    automatically or if it is not related to movements out of
 3651  *    the stock. For example, if a stock transfer is posted, the
 3652  *    system creates a material document with two lines: Out of
 3653  *    the old stock (accepted) and into the transfer stock (rejected,
 3654  *    because the material is not yet visible in the target location).
 3655  *    When the movement into the stock is posted, this is accepted.
 3656  * 2) Valuated stock:
 3657  *    a) Movements within a single plant (MA05, MA06 =
 3658  *       movement types 313-316) are ignored.
 3659  *    b) The moving of material out of a plant (303/304)
 3660  *       is counted and valuated in the emitting plant and
 3661  *       the target plant. The moving in
 3662  *       (305/306) is ignored, because
 3663  *       the valuated stock appears in the target at the

 4851  *----------------------------------------------------------------------*
 4852  *    F0410_FIELDCAT
 4853  *----------------------------------------------------------------------*
 4854
 4855  FORM f0410_fieldcat
 4856           USING  l_f_check
 4857                  l_f_no_out   TYPE      slis_fieldcat_main-no_out.
 4858
 4859    DATA : l_f_continue(01) TYPE c,
 4860           l_f_type(01)     TYPE c,
 4861           l_f_fieldname    TYPE      stype_fields.
 4862
 4863    FIELD-SYMBOLS : <l_fs>.
 4864
 4865    IF  l_f_check = c_take.
 4866  *   take this entry without check
 4867      MOVE  'X'                TO  l_f_continue.
 4868    ELSE.
 4869  *   create key and look for fieldname
 4870      CONCATENATE              g_s_fieldcat-ref_tabname
 4871                               '~'
 4872                               g_s_fieldcat-fieldname
 4873                               INTO l_f_fieldname.
 4874
 4875      READ TABLE g_t_mseg_fields         INTO g_s_mseg_fields
 4876                               WITH KEY
 4877                               fieldname = l_f_fieldname
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
21.07.26 S2A      Program RM07MLBD                              Page     83
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 4878                               BINARY SEARCH.
 4879
 4880      IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
 4881        MOVE  'X'              TO  l_f_continue.
 4882      ELSE.
 4883  *     additional fields are displayed in wrong format :     "n480130
 4884  *     clear the working area for the field catalog when     "n480130
 4885  *     the current field should not be processed             "n480130
 4886        CLEAR                  g_s_fieldcat.                  "n480130
 4887        CLEAR                  l_f_continue.
 4888      ENDIF.
 4889    ENDIF.
 4890
 4891  * append entry to field catalog if field is in structure
 4892  * else leave this routine
 4893    IF l_f_continue IS INITIAL.
 4894      CLEAR                    g_s_fieldcat.
 4895      EXIT.
 4896    ENDIF.
 4897
 4898    IF  NOT l_f_no_out IS INITIAL.
 4899      MOVE  l_f_no_out         TO  g_s_fieldcat-no_out.
 4900    ENDIF.
 4901
 4902    ADD  : 1                   TO  g_f_col_pos.
 4903    MOVE : g_f_col_pos         TO  g_s_fieldcat-col_pos,
 4904           g_f_tabname         TO  g_s_fieldcat-tabname.
 4905    APPEND g_s_fieldcat        TO  fieldcat.
 4906
 4907  * create the table with the fields who will be enriched with colors
 4908  * and sign
 4909    IF  g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  'MENGE'  OR
 4910        g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  'MEINS'  OR
 4911        g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  'DMBTR'  OR
 4912        g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  'WAERS'  OR
 4913        g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  'ERFMG'  OR
 4914        g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  'ERFME'  OR
 4915
 4916        g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  'BPMNG'  OR
 4917        g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  'BPRME'  OR
 4918        g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  'BSTMG'  OR
 4919        g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  'BSTME'  OR
 4920        g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  'EXBWR'  OR
 4921        g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  'VKWRT'  OR
 4922
 4923        g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  'EXVKW'  OR
 4924        g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  'VKWRA'  OR
 4925        g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  'LSMNG'  OR
 4926        g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  'LSMEH'  OR
 4927        g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  'SHKZG'.
 4928
 4929  *   look for the type of this field
 4930      CONCATENATE              g_s_fieldcat-ref_tabname
 4931                               '-'
 4932                               g_s_fieldcat-fieldname
 4933                               INTO l_f_fieldname.
 4934
 4935      ASSIGN  (l_f_fieldname)  TO <l_fs>.
 4936
 4937      IF  sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
 4938        DESCRIBE FIELD <l_fs>    TYPE  l_f_type.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
21.07.26 S2A      Program RM07MLBD                              Page     84
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 4939        MOVE : g_s_fieldcat-fieldname
 4940                               TO  g_t_color_fields-fieldname,
 4941             l_f_type          TO  g_t_color_fields-type.
 4942        APPEND                 g_t_color_fields.
 4943      ENDIF.
 4944    ENDIF.
 4945    LOG-POINT ID /cwm/enh SUBKEY to_upper( sy-tcode && '\/CWM/APPL_MM_RM07
       MLBD\EHP605_RM07MLBD_16\' && sy-cprog ) FIELDS /cwm/cl_enh_layer=>get_fi
       eld( ).
 4946  *
 4947    IF  g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  '/CWM/MENGE'  OR
 4948        g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  '/CWM/MEINS'  OR
 4949        g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  '/CWM/ERFMG'  OR
 4950        g_s_fieldcat-fieldname  =  '/CWM/ERFME'.
 4951  *   look for the type of this field
 4952      CONCATENATE              g_s_fieldcat-ref_tabname
 4953                               '-'
 4954                               g_s_fieldcat-fieldname
 4955                               INTO l_f_fieldname.
 4956
 4957      ASSIGN  (l_f_fieldname)  TO <l_fs>.
 4958
 4959      IF  sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
 4960        DESCRIBE FIELD <l_fs>    TYPE  l_f_type.
 4961        MOVE : g_s_fieldcat-fieldname
 4962                               TO  g_t_color_fields-fieldname,
 4963             l_f_type          TO  g_t_color_fields-type.
 4964        APPEND                 g_t_color_fields.
 4965      ENDIF.
 4966    ENDIF.

 5363  *&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
 5364  *&      Form  USER_COMMAND                                             *

 5366
 5367  FORM user_command                                           "#EC CALLED
 5368                     USING     r_ucomm      LIKE  sy-ucomm
 5369                               rs_selfield  TYPE  slis_selfield.
 5370
 5371    TYPES: BEGIN OF ty_s_sel,
 5372             mblnr LIKE  mseg-mblnr,
 5373             mjahr LIKE  mseg-mjahr,
 5374             zeile LIKE  mseg-zeile,
 5375             bukrs LIKE  mseg-bukrs,
 5376             belnr LIKE  mseg-belnr,
 5377             gjahr LIKE  mseg-gjahr,
 5378           END OF ty_s_sel,
 5379
 5380           ty_t_sel TYPE ty_s_sel OCCURS 0.
 5381
 5382    DATA: l_value(10) TYPE c,                                 "n1583816
 5383          ls_sel      TYPE ty_s_sel,
 5384          lt_sel      TYPE ty_t_sel,
 5385          l_lines     LIKE sy-tabix,
 5386          ls_fc       TYPE slis_fieldcat_alv,
 5387          lt_fc       TYPE slis_t_fieldcat_alv,
 5388          ls_selfield TYPE slis_selfield,
 5389          l_fi_doc    TYPE c  LENGTH 1.                       "n1511550
 5390
 5391  * Unfortunately the output list of this report consists
 5392  * of several ALVs, one started at the end-event of the other.
 5393  * This abstrucse programming style was chosen to create a list
 5394  * layout similar to the one in release 3.1. Now this causes a severe
 5395  * problem: When selecting a line, we do not know which ALV (and there-
 5396  * for which line in table IMSEG) has been selected. We can only use
 5397  * the value of the selected field to access the data-table.
 5398  * In case of ambiguities, a popup has to be transmitted where the
 5399  * user has to reselect the document he wants to see. This is
 5400  * difficult to understand, if you do not know the problems of
 5401  * programming ABAP.
 5402
 5403    CASE r_ucomm.
 5404      WHEN '9PBP'.
 5405  *     Get line of IMSEG which "look" like the one selected
 5406        l_value = rs_selfield-value.
 5407        CHECK NOT l_value IS INITIAL.                         "204872
 5408        CALL FUNCTION 'CONVERSION_EXIT_ALPHA_INPUT'              "n1604106
 5409          EXPORTING                                              "n1604106
 5410            input  = l_value                                     "n1604106
 5411          IMPORTING                                              "n1604106
 5412            output = l_value.                                    "n1604106
 5413        IF rs_selfield-sel_tab_field = 'G_T_BELEGE-MBLNR' OR
 5414           rs_selfield-sel_tab_field = 'G_T_BELEGE1-MBLNR'.
 5415          LOOP AT g_t_mseg_lean          INTO  g_s_mseg_lean
 5416                                         WHERE mblnr = l_value.
 5417            ls_sel-mblnr = g_s_mseg_lean-mblnr.
 5418            ls_sel-mjahr = g_s_mseg_lean-mjahr.
 5419            ls_sel-zeile = g_s_mseg_lean-zeile.
 5420            COLLECT ls_sel INTO lt_sel.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
21.07.26 S2A      Program RM07MLBD                              Page     92
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 5421          ENDLOOP.
 5422
 5423        ELSEIF rs_selfield-sel_tab_field = 'G_T_BELEGE-BELNR' OR
 5424               rs_selfield-sel_tab_field = 'G_T_BELEGE1-BELNR'.
 5425          l_fi_doc = 'X'.
 5426          LOOP AT g_t_mseg_lean          INTO  g_s_mseg_lean
 5427                                         WHERE belnr = l_value.
 5428            ls_sel-belnr = g_s_mseg_lean-belnr.
 5429            ls_sel-gjahr = g_s_mseg_lean-gjahr.
 5430            ls_sel-bukrs = g_s_mseg_lean-bukrs.
 5431            COLLECT ls_sel INTO lt_sel.
 5432          ENDLOOP.
 5433
 5434        ENDIF.
 5435        SORT lt_sel BY mjahr mblnr zeile bukrs belnr gjahr.
 5436  *     Read first line. If L_LINES = 1, LS_SEL is filled properly.
 5437        READ TABLE lt_sel INTO ls_sel INDEX 1.
 5438        DESCRIBE TABLE lt_sel LINES l_lines.
 5439  *     If no line found, the cursor was not on a useful value.
 5440        IF l_lines = 0.
 5441          MESSAGE s270.
 5442          EXIT.
 5443        ENDIF.
 5444  *     If more than one line found, it gets difficult. We send a popup
 5445  *     where the user may select a single line.
 5446        IF l_lines > 1.
 5447  *       Create fieldcatalog
 5448          DEFINE fc_add.
 5449            ls_fc-fieldname     = &1.
 5450            ls_fc-ref_tabname   = &2.
 5451            ls_fc-ref_fieldname = &3.
 5452            APPEND ls_fc TO lt_fc.
 5453          END-OF-DEFINITION.
 5454          CLEAR ls_sel.
 5455          IF l_fi_doc IS INITIAL.
 5456            fc_add 'MBLNR' 'MKPF' 'MBLNR'.
 5457            fc_add 'MJAHR' 'MKPF' 'MJAHR'.
 5458            fc_add 'ZEILE' 'MSEG' 'ZEILE'.
 5459          ELSE.
 5460            fc_add 'BUKRS' 'BKPF' 'BUKRS'.
 5461            fc_add 'BELNR' 'BKPF' 'BELNR'.
 5462            fc_add 'GJAHR' 'BKPF' 'GJAHR'.
 5463          ENDIF.
 5464
 5465          CALL FUNCTION 'REUSE_ALV_POPUP_TO_SELECT'
 5466            EXPORTING
 5467              i_zebra     = 'X'
 5468              i_tabname   = 'LT_SEL'
 5469              it_fieldcat = lt_fc
 5470            IMPORTING
 5471              es_selfield = ls_selfield
 5472            TABLES
 5473              t_outtab    = lt_sel.
 5474  *       Read table with the unique index.
 5475          READ TABLE lt_sel INTO ls_sel INDEX ls_selfield-tabindex.
 5476          IF sy-subrc <> 0.
 5477            EXIT.
 5478          ENDIF.
 5479        ENDIF.
 5480
 5481  *     read and save the user parameters before calling
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
21.07.26 S2A      Program RM07MLBD                              Page     93
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 5482  *     transaction MIGO or FB03
 5483        PERFORM                user_parameters_save.
 5484
 5485  *     Now call the corresponding application. LS_SEL is always filled
 5486  *     correctly.
 5487        IF l_fi_doc IS INITIAL.
 5488
 5489  *     call the display transcation MIGO for the MM document "TEST
 5490          CALL FUNCTION 'MIGO_DIALOG'                       "n547170
 5491            EXPORTING                                       "n547170
 5492              i_action            = 'A04'                   "n547170
 5493              i_refdoc            = 'R02'                   "n547170
 5494              i_notree            = 'X'                     "n547170
 5495              i_no_auth_check     = ' '                     "n547170
 5496              i_deadend           = 'X'                     "n547170
 5497              i_skip_first_screen = 'X'                     "n547170
 5498              i_okcode            = 'OK_GO'                 "n547170
 5499              i_mblnr             = ls_sel-mblnr            "n547170
 5500              i_mjahr             = ls_sel-mjahr            "n547170
 5501              i_zeile             = ls_sel-zeile.           "n547170
 5502        ELSE.
 5503          SET PARAMETER ID 'BLN' FIELD ls_sel-belnr.
 5504          SET PARAMETER ID 'BUK' FIELD ls_sel-bukrs.
 5505          SET PARAMETER ID 'GJR' FIELD ls_sel-gjahr.
 5506          CALL TRANSACTION 'FB03'               "#EC CI_CALLTA  "n1511550
 5507                               AND SKIP FIRST SCREEN.         "n1511550
 5508        ENDIF.
 5509
 5510  *     restore the former user parameters
 5511        PERFORM                user_parameters_restore.
 5512
 5513    ENDCASE.
 5514
 5515  ENDFORM.                               " USER_COMMAND

 5735  * calculate the offsets for the list header
 5736
 5737  FORM calculate_offsets.
 5738
 5739  *  working area
 5740    DATA : l_text(132)         TYPE c.
 5741
 5742  * get the maximal length of the text elements to be used
 5743    PERFORM  get_max_text_length USING  TEXT-020.
 5744    PERFORM  get_max_text_length USING  TEXT-021.
 5745    PERFORM  get_max_text_length USING  TEXT-022.
 5746    PERFORM  get_max_text_length USING  TEXT-023.

 5756      WRITE : datum-low        TO  g_date_line_from-datum DD/MM/YYYY.
 5757      CONDENSE                 g_date_line_from.
 5758      PERFORM  get_max_text_length USING  g_date_line_from.
 5759
 5760      MOVE  TEXT-005           TO  g_text_line-text.
 5761      PERFORM  get_max_text_length USING  g_text_line.
 5762
 5763      MOVE  TEXT-006           TO  g_text_line.
 5764      PERFORM  get_max_text_length USING  g_text_line.

 5767      WRITE : datum-high       TO  g_date_line_to-datum DD/MM/YYYY.
 5768      CONDENSE                 g_date_line_to.
 5769    ELSE.
 5770  *     stocks, quantities, and values
 5771      MOVE   TEXT-008          TO  g_date_line_from-text.
 5772      WRITE : datum-low        TO  g_date_line_from-datum DD/MM/YYYY.
 5773      CONDENSE                 g_date_line_from.
 5774
 5775  *     the start and end dates were shown incorrectly in the "n856424
 5776  *     headlines in the mode valuated stock                  "n856424
 5777      PERFORM  get_max_text_length USING  g_date_line_from.   "n856424
 5778
 5779      MOVE  TEXT-030           TO  g_text_line-text.
 5780      PERFORM  get_max_text_length USING  g_text_line.
 5781
 5782      MOVE  TEXT-031           TO  g_text_line-text.
 5783      PERFORM  get_max_text_length USING  g_text_line.
 5784
 5785      MOVE   TEXT-008          TO  g_date_line_to-text.

  147  * customizing for the selection of remaining BSIM entries   "n497992
  148  * ( FI document ) without matching MSEG ( MM document )     "n497992
  149  * like price changes, account adjustments, etc...           "n497992
  150  *                                                           "n497992
  151  * value ' ' : (default) take all remaining BSIM entries     "n497992
  152  * value 'X' : take only the remaining BSIM entries when     "n497992
  153  *             when the original BSEG entry contains the     "n497992
  154  *             transaction key ( KTOSL ) 'BSX'               "n497992
  155  *             this mode will cost performance               "n497992
  156    data : G_cust_bseg_bsx(01) type c    value ' '.           "n497992
  157  * data : G_cust_bseg_bsx(01) type c    value 'X'.           "n497992
  158
  159  *----------------------------------------------------------------------*

  162  *                                                           "n497992
  163  * value ' ' : (default) do not consider tied empties        "n497992
  164  * value 'X' : consider tied empties materials with their    "n497992
  165  *             special rules in the inventory management     "n497992
  166  *             this mode will cost performance               "n497992
  167    data : G_cust_tied_empties(01)  type c    value ' '.      "n497992
  168  * data : G_cust_tied_empties(01)  type c    value 'X'.      "n547170

  901  *&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
  902  *&      Form  TABELLEN_LESEN
  903  *&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
  904  *       Lesen der Materialkurztexte (Tabelle MAKT),                    *
  905  *       der Mengeneinheiten (Tabelle MARA) und                         *
  906  *       Mengen- und Wertfortschreibung zum Material (Tabelle T134M)    *
  907  *       (Letzteres ist zum Aussortieren der unbewerteten bzw.          *
  908  *       kontierten Warenbewegungen notwendig)                          *
  909  *----------------------------------------------------------------------*
  910
  911  FORM tabellen_lesen.
  912
  913    IF  NOT g_t_mat_key[] IS INITIAL.                         "n451923
  914  ENHANCEMENT-SECTION ehp605_tabellen_lesen_01 SPOTS es_rm07mlbd .
  915  LOG-POINT ID /cwm/enh SUBKEY to_upper( sy-tcode && '\/CWM/APPL_MM_RM07ML
       BD\EHP605_TABELLEN_LESEN_01\' && sy-cprog ) FIELDS /cwm/cl_enh_layer=>ge
       t_field( ).
  916  *   select the material masters
  917  PERFORM hdb_check_table USING 'MARA' ''.            "1791598/1710850
  918  SELECT matnr meins mtart
  919         /cwm/valum                                           "1734569
  920         /cwm/xcwmat FROM mara CONNECTION (dbcon)     "1791598/1710850
  921                 INTO CORRESPONDING FIELDS OF TABLE imara
  922                 FOR ALL ENTRIES IN g_t_mat_key
  923                           WHERE  matnr  =  g_t_mat_key-matnr.
  924  END-ENHANCEMENT-SECTION.
  925
  926  *   select the short text for all materials
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
21.07.26 S2A      Include RM07MLBD_FORM_01                      Page    147
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

  927  *   take only the necessary fields                          "n451923
  928      PERFORM hdb_check_table USING 'MAKT' ''.                "n1710850
  929      SELECT matnr maktx       FROM makt CONNECTION (dbcon)   "n1710850
  930           INTO CORRESPONDING FIELDS OF TABLE g_t_makt        "n451923
  931                     FOR ALL ENTRIES IN g_t_mat_key
  932                     WHERE  matnr = g_t_mat_key-matnr
  933                       AND  spras = sy-langu.
  934
  935      SORT  imara              BY  matnr.                     "n451923
  936      SORT  g_t_makt           BY  matnr.                     "n451923
  937      FREE                     g_t_mat_key.
  938    ENDIF.
  939
  940    DATA: BEGIN OF k1 OCCURS 0,
  941            mtart LIKE t134m-mtart,
  942          END OF k1.
  943    REFRESH k1.
  944
  945    LOOP AT imara.
  946      k1-mtart = imara-mtart.
  947      COLLECT k1.
  948    ENDLOOP.
  949
  950    IF  NOT k1[] IS INITIAL.                                  "n451923
  951      SELECT * FROM t134m                                 "#EC CI_GENBUFF
  952             INTO CORRESPONDING FIELDS OF TABLE it134m
  953             FOR ALL ENTRIES IN k1         WHERE mtart = k1-mtart
  954                                           AND   bwkey IN g_ra_bwkey.
  955    ENDIF.                                                    "n451923
  956
  957    LOOP AT it134m.
  958  *   read table organ with key bwkey = it134m-bwkey.
  959      PERFORM  f9300_read_organ
  960                     USING     c_bwkey     it134m-bwkey.
  961
  962      IF sy-subrc NE 0.
  963        DELETE it134m.
  964      ENDIF.
  965    ENDLOOP.
  966
  967  * To find postings with valuation string, but without relevance for
  968  * the valuated stock, Big-G recommended this logic:
  969  * Take lines from MSEG where for the combination BUSTW/XAUTO=XBGBB
  970  * there is an entry in T156W with key BSX.
  971    SELECT bustw xbgbb FROM t156w
  972                       INTO CORRESPONDING FIELDS OF TABLE it156w
  973                       WHERE vorsl = 'BSX'.
  974    SORT it156w BY bustw xbgbb.
  975    DELETE ADJACENT DUPLICATES FROM it156w.
  976    DELETE it156w WHERE bustw = space.
  977
  978  ENDFORM.                               " TABELLEN_LESEN
  979
  980  *&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
  981  *&      Form  UNBEWERTET_WEG
  982  *&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
  983  *       Löschen der unbewerteten Materialien aus der internen          *
  984  *       Tabelle IMBEW
  985  *----------------------------------------------------------------------*
  986
  987  FORM unbewertet_weg.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
21.07.26 S2A      Include RM07MLBD_FORM_01                      Page    148
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

  988
  989    SORT  it134m               BY bwkey mtart.                "n451923
  990                                                              "n450764
  991  * delete the materials in plants without valuation          "n450764
  992    LOOP AT g_t_mbew           INTO  g_s_mbew.                "n450764
  993      READ TABLE imara                                        "n450764
  994                     WITH KEY matnr = g_s_mbew-matnr          "n450764

 1148        FROM mmim_rep_ln_lim
 1149        WHERE report = 'RM07MLBD'
 1150          AND tabname = 'MSEG_LEAN'.
 1151
 1152      CLEAR lv_zaehler.
 1153      LOOP AT g_t_mseg_lean    INTO  g_s_mseg_lean
 1154                               WHERE budat > datum-high.
 1155        MOVE-CORRESPONDING g_s_mseg_lean TO imsweg.
 1156        IF lv_limit > 0.
 1157  * Check entries before the memory for internal table is to small
 1158          ADD 1 TO lv_zaehler.
 1159          IF lv_zaehler > lv_limit.
 1160            MESSAGE i555(m7).
 1161  * Too many records selected. Not enough memory. Restrict your selection
 1162            SUBMIT rm07mlbd VIA SELECTION-SCREEN .
 1163          ENDIF.
 1164        ENDIF.

 3420  *    create_headline                                        "n599218
 3421  *-----------------------------------------------------------"n599218
 3422                                                              "n599218
 3423  FORM create_headline.                                       "n599218
 3424                                                              "n599218
 3425    DATA : l_offset TYPE i,                                   "n599218
 3426           l_strlen TYPE i.                                   "n599218
 3427                                                              "n599218
 3428  * get the length of the title                               "n599218
 3429    COMPUTE  l_strlen          = strlen( sy-title ).          "n599218
 3430                                                              "n599218
 3431    IF  bwbst IS INITIAL.                                     "n599218
 3432  *   stocks only --> small line with 77 bytes                "n599218
 3433      IF      l_strlen   =  59.                               "n599218
 3434        MOVE : sy-title        TO  g_s_header_77-title.       "n599218
 3435      ELSEIF  l_strlen   >  59.                               "n599218
 3436        MOVE : sy-title        TO  g_s_header_77-title,       "n599218
 3437               '...'          TO  g_s_header_77-title+56(03). "n599218
 3438      ELSE.                                                   "n599218
 3439        COMPUTE  l_offset      =  ( 59 - l_strlen ) / 2.      "n599218
 3440        MOVE : sy-title     TO  g_s_header_77-title+l_offset. "n599218
 3441      ENDIF.                                                  "n599218
 3442                                                              "n599218
 3443      WRITE : sy-datlo DD/MM/YYYY   TO  g_s_header_77-date.   "n599218
 3444    ELSE.                                                     "n599218
 3445  *   stocks and values --> wide line with 91 bytes           "n599218
 3446      IF      l_strlen   =  73.                               "n599218
 3447        MOVE : sy-title        TO  g_s_header_91-title.       "n599218

 3967      USING
 3968            et_mbew TYPE stab_mbew.
 3969
 3970    TYPES:
 3971      BEGIN OF lts_valuation_area,
 3972        bwkey TYPE bwkey,
 3973        bukrs TYPE bukrs,
 3974        bwmod TYPE bwmod,
 3975      END OF lts_valuation_area,
 3976
 3977      BEGIN OF lts_account,
 3978        ktopl TYPE t030r-ktopl,
 3979

 3981        bklas TYPE t030-bklas,
 3982
 3983        saknr TYPE t030-konts,
 3984      END OF lts_account,
 3985
 3986      ltt_account TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF lts_account.
 3987
 3988
 3989
 3990    DATA:
 3991      lt_organ       LIKE g_t_organ[].
 3992
 3993
 3994  * table G_T_ORGAN should be already filled in; otherwise settings for al
       l
 3995  * charts of accounts need to be read which is very time consuming
 3996    lt_organ = g_t_organ[].
 3997    SORT lt_organ BY ktopl bwmod.
 3998    DELETE ADJACENT DUPLICATES FROM lt_organ COMPARING ktopl bwmod.
 3999    IF lt_organ IS INITIAL.
 4000      MESSAGE s480.
 4001      PERFORM anforderungsbild.
 4002    ENDIF.
 4003
 4004  * read Valuation Areas with Valuation Grouping Code
 4005    DATA:

       nd organizations
 4023    DATA:

 4046      AND account~konts IN hkont.

 4050    FROM
 4051      t030r AS standart_account_rule
 4052    INTO CORRESPONDING FIELDS OF TABLE
 4053      lt_rules

 4055      lt_organ

 4058      AND standart_account_rule~ktosl EQ 'BSX'
 4059    ORDER BY
 4060      PRIMARY KEY.
 4061
 4062
 4063  * determine if rules restrict selection by valuation grouping codes or v
       aluation classes
 4064    DATA:
 4065      lv_bklas_restricted TYPE abap_bool,
 4066      lv_bwmod_restricted TYPE abap_bool.
 4067    FIELD-SYMBOLS:

 4071
 4072    READ TABLE lt_rules WITH KEY xbwmo = 'X' TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS.
 4073    IF sy-subrc = 0.
 4074      lv_bwmod_restricted = 'X'.
 4075    ELSE.
 4076      lv_bwmod_restricted = ''.
 4077    ENDIF.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
21.07.26 S2A      Include RM07MLBD_FORM_01                      Page    202

 4078
 4079    READ TABLE lt_rules WITH KEY xbkla = 'X' TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS.
 4080    IF sy-subrc = 0.
 4081      lv_bklas_restricted = 'X'.
 4082    ELSE.
 4083      lv_bklas_restricted = ''.
 4084    ENDIF.
 4085
 4086    g_ra_bwkey-sign = 'I'.
 4087    g_ra_bwkey-option = 'EQ'.
 4088
 4089  * if selection is restricted by valuation grouping code(BWMOD) also rest
       rict valuation area selection
 4090    IF lv_bwmod_restricted = abap_true.
 4091      CLEAR g_ra_bwkey-low.
 4092      LOOP AT lt_rules ASSIGNING <fs_standart_account_rule> WHERE XBWMO =
       'X'.
 4093          LOOP AT lt_accounts ASSIGNING <fs_selected_account> WHERE ktopl
       = <fs_standart_account_rule>-ktopl.
 4094            LOOP AT lt_valuation_areas ASSIGNING <fs_valuation_area> WHERE
        bwmod = <fs_selected_account>-bwmod.
 4095              g_ra_bwkey-low = <fs_valuation_area>-bwkey.
 4096              APPEND g_ra_bwkey TO g_ra_bwkey.
 4097          ENDLOOP.
 4098          ENDLOOP.
 4099      ENDLOOP.
 4100    ENDIF.
 4101    DELETE ADJACENT DUPLICATES FROM g_ra_bwkey.
 4102
 4103
 4104    IF lt_accounts IS INITIAL.
 4105      MESSAGE s289.
 4106  *   no data contained in the selection
 4107      PERFORM anforderungsbild.
 4108    ENDIF.

 4320          WITH KEY bklas = <fs_full_mbew>-bklas TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS.
 4321

 4325          WITH KEY bwmod = <fs_full_mbew>-bwmod TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS.
 4326

 4330          WHERE bklas = '' AND bwmod = ''.

 4332      ENDIF.
 4333
 4334      IF sy-subrc <> 0.
 4335        CONTINUE.
 4336      ENDIF.

 4339      MOVE-CORRESPONDING <fs_full_mbew> TO <fs_mbew>.

 4346  *&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
 4347  *&      Form  GET_ACC_DET
 4348  *&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
 4349  *       Get G/L account from current account determination settings
 4350  *----------------------------------------------------------------------*
 4351  FORM get_acc_det  CHANGING cs_accdet  TYPE stype_accdet.
 4352
 4353    TYPES:
 4354      BEGIN OF ltt_acc,
 4355        bklas LIKE t030-bklas,
 4356        bwmod LIKE t030-bwmod,
 4357        ktopl LIKE t030-ktopl,
 4358        hkont LIKE t030-konts,
 4359      END OF ltt_acc.
 4360
 4361    STATICS:
 4362      lt_acc TYPE HASHED TABLE OF ltt_acc WITH UNIQUE KEY bklas bwmod ktop
       l.
 4363    DATA:
 4364      ls_acc TYPE ltt_acc.
 4365
 4366  * get organizational data
 4367    PERFORM f9300_read_organ
 4368      USING c_werks cs_accdet-werks.
 4369    CHECK g_s_organ-bukrs = cs_accdet-bukrs.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
21.07.26 S2A      Include RM07MLBD_FORM_01                      Page    207
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 4370    cs_accdet-bwkey = g_s_organ-bwkey.
 4371    cs_accdet-ktopl = g_s_organ-ktopl.
 4372    cs_accdet-bwmod = g_s_organ-bwmod.
 4373
 4374  * check for special stock that is valuated in MBEW
 4375    IF ( cs_accdet-sobkz = 'Q' OR cs_accdet-sobkz = 'E' ) AND
 4376       cs_accdet-kzbws = 'A'.
 4377      CLEAR: cs_accdet-sobkz.
 4378    ENDIF.
 4379    IF cs_accdet-sobkz = 'O' AND cs_accdet-xobew IS INITIAL.
 4380      CLEAR: cs_accdet-sobkz.
 4381    ENDIF.
 4382
 4383  * get special stock data
 4384  * (if not filled yet via customer's enhancement of type STYPE_MB5B_ADD)
 4385    CASE cs_accdet-sobkz.
 4386      WHEN 'Q'.
 4387        IF cs_accdet-mat_pspnr IS INITIAL.
 4388          PERFORM hdb_check_table USING 'MSEG' ''.            "n1710850
 4389          SELECT SINGLE mat_pspnr FROM nsdm_v_mseg CONNECTION (dbcon) "n17
       10850
 4390            INTO cs_accdet-mat_pspnr
 4391            WHERE mblnr = cs_accdet-mblnr
 4392              AND mjahr = cs_accdet-mjahr
 4393              AND zeile = cs_accdet-zeile.
 4394        ENDIF.
 4395        CLEAR: cs_accdet-mat_kdauf, cs_accdet-mat_kdpos, cs_accdet-lifnr.
 4396      WHEN 'E'.
 4397        IF cs_accdet-mat_kdauf IS INITIAL OR cs_accdet-mat_kdpos IS INITIA
       L.
 4398          PERFORM hdb_check_table USING 'MSEG' ''.            "n1710850
 4399          SELECT SINGLE mat_kdauf mat_kdpos FROM nsdm_v_mseg CONNECTION (d
       bcon) "n1710850
 4400            INTO (cs_accdet-mat_kdauf, cs_accdet-mat_kdpos)
 4401            WHERE mblnr = cs_accdet-mblnr
 4402              AND mjahr = cs_accdet-mjahr
 4403              AND zeile = cs_accdet-zeile.
 4404        ENDIF.
 4405        CLEAR: cs_accdet-mat_pspnr, cs_accdet-lifnr.
 4406      WHEN 'O'.
 4407        IF cs_accdet-lifnr IS INITIAL.
 4408          PERFORM hdb_check_table USING 'MSEG' ''.            "n1710850
 4409          SELECT SINGLE lifnr FROM nsdm_v_mseg CONNECTION (dbcon) "n171085
       0
 4410            INTO cs_accdet-lifnr
 4411            WHERE mblnr = cs_accdet-mblnr
 4412              AND mjahr = cs_accdet-mjahr
 4413              AND zeile = cs_accdet-zeile.
 4414        ENDIF.
 4415        CLEAR: cs_accdet-mat_kdauf, cs_accdet-mat_kdpos, cs_accdet-mat_psp
       nr.
 4416      WHEN OTHERS.
 4417        CLEAR: cs_accdet-mat_kdauf, cs_accdet-mat_kdpos,
 4418               cs_accdet-mat_pspnr, cs_accdet-lifnr.
 4419    ENDCASE.
 4420
 4421  * get valuation class
 4422    PERFORM get_bklas CHANGING cs_accdet.
 4423
 4424  * get G/L account
 4425    READ TABLE lt_acc INTO ls_acc
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
21.07.26 S2A      Include RM07MLBD_FORM_01                      Page    208
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 4426      WITH TABLE KEY bklas = cs_accdet-bklas
 4427                     bwmod = cs_accdet-bwmod
 4428                     ktopl = cs_accdet-ktopl.
 4429    IF sy-subrc = 0.
 4430      cs_accdet-hkont = ls_acc-hkont.
 4431    ELSE.
 4432      CALL FUNCTION 'MR_ACCOUNT_ASSIGNMENT'
 4433        EXPORTING
 4434          bewertungsklasse       = cs_accdet-bklas
 4435          bewertung_modif        = cs_accdet-bwmod
 4436          kontenplan             = cs_accdet-ktopl
 4437          soll_haben_kennzeichen = 'S'
 4438          vorgangsschluessel     = 'BSX'
 4439        IMPORTING
 4440          konto                  = cs_accdet-hkont
 4441        EXCEPTIONS
 4442          OTHERS                 = 5.
 4443      IF sy-subrc <> 0.
 4444        CLEAR cs_accdet-hkont.
 4445      ENDIF.
 4446      ls_acc-bklas = cs_accdet-bklas.
 4447      ls_acc-bwmod = cs_accdet-bwmod.
 4448      ls_acc-ktopl = cs_accdet-ktopl.
 4449      ls_acc-hkont = cs_accdet-hkont.
 4450      INSERT ls_acc INTO TABLE lt_acc.
 4451    ENDIF.
 4452
 4453  ENDFORM.                    " GET_ACC_DET
 4454  *&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
 4455  *&      Form  GET_BKLAS
 4456  *&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
 4457  *      Get valuation class from current settings
 4458  *----------------------------------------------------------------------*
 4459  FORM get_bklas  CHANGING cs_accdet  TYPE stype_accdet.
 4460
 4461    TYPES:
 4462      BEGIN OF ltt_bklas,
 4463        matnr     LIKE mbew-matnr,
 4464        bwkey     LIKE mbew-bwkey,
 4465        bwtar     LIKE mbew-bwtar,
 4466        sobkz     LIKE qbew-sobkz,
 4467        mat_pspnr LIKE qbew-pspnr,
 4468        mat_kdauf LIKE ebew-vbeln,
 4469        mat_kdpos LIKE ebew-posnr,
 4470        lifnr     LIKE obew-lifnr,
 4471        bklas     LIKE mbew-bklas,
 4472      END OF ltt_bklas.
 4473
 4474    STATICS:
 4475      lt_bklas TYPE HASHED TABLE OF ltt_bklas WITH UNIQUE KEY matnr bwkey
 4476        bwtar sobkz mat_pspnr mat_kdauf mat_kdpos lifnr.
 4477    DATA:
 4478      ls_bklas TYPE ltt_bklas.
 4479
 4480    READ TABLE lt_bklas INTO ls_bklas
 4481      WITH TABLE KEY matnr     = cs_accdet-matnr
 4482                     bwkey     = cs_accdet-bwkey
 4483                     bwtar     = cs_accdet-bwtar
 4484                     sobkz     = cs_accdet-sobkz
 4485                     mat_pspnr = cs_accdet-mat_pspnr
 4486                     mat_kdauf = cs_accdet-mat_kdauf
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
21.07.26 S2A      Include RM07MLBD_FORM_01                      Page    209
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

 4487                     mat_kdpos = cs_accdet-mat_kdpos
 4488                     lifnr     = cs_accdet-lifnr.
 4489    IF sy-subrc = 0.
 4490      cs_accdet-bklas = ls_bklas-bklas.
 4491    ELSE.
 4492      CASE cs_accdet-sobkz.
 4493        WHEN 'Q'.
 4494          PERFORM hdb_check_table USING 'QBEW' ''.            "n1710850
 4495          SELECT SINGLE bklas FROM qbew CONNECTION (dbcon)    "n1710850
 4496            INTO cs_accdet-bklas
 4497            WHERE matnr = cs_accdet-matnr
 4498              AND bwkey = cs_accdet-bwkey
 4499              AND bwtar = cs_accdet-bwtar
 4500              AND sobkz = cs_accdet-sobkz
 4501              AND pspnr = cs_accdet-mat_pspnr.
 4502        WHEN 'E'.
 4503          PERFORM hdb_check_table USING 'EBEW' ''.            "n1710850
 4504          SELECT SINGLE bklas FROM ebew CONNECTION (dbcon)    "n1710850
 4505            INTO cs_accdet-bklas
 4506            WHERE matnr = cs_accdet-matnr
 4507              AND bwkey = cs_accdet-bwkey
 4508              AND bwtar = cs_accdet-bwtar
 4509              AND sobkz = cs_accdet-sobkz
 4510              AND vbeln = cs_accdet-mat_kdauf
 4511              AND posnr = cs_accdet-mat_kdpos.

 4514          SELECT SINGLE bklas FROM obew CONNECTION (dbcon)    "n1710850

       MLBD\EHP605_RM07MLBD_FORM_02_01\' && sy-cprog ) FIELDS /cwm/cl_enh_layer
       =>get_field( ).
  198                                                              "n599218
  199  * process table BESTAND                                     "n599218
  200    LOOP AT bestand.                                          "n599218
  201      CLEAR                    l_category.                    "n599218
  202                                                              "n599218
  203  *   determine the category of each entry                    "n599218
  204
  205      IF  bestand-soll      IS INITIAL    AND
  206          bestand-haben     IS INITIAL    AND
  207          bestand-/cwm/soll      IS INITIAL    AND
  208          bestand-/cwm/haben     IS INITIAL    AND
  209          bestand-sollwert  IS INITIAL    AND
  210          bestand-habenwert IS INITIAL.
  211  *     material without movements
  212
  213        IF  bestand-endmenge  IS INITIAL  AND
  214            bestand-anfmenge  IS INITIAL  AND
  215            bestand-/cwm/endmenge  IS INITIAL  AND
  216            bestand-/cwm/anfmenge  IS INITIAL  AND
  217            bestand-anfwert   IS INITIAL  AND
  218            bestand-endwert   IS INITIAL.
  219  *       material without movements / no stocks
  220          MOVE  'PA_NDZER'     TO  l_category.
  221        ELSE.
  222  *       material without movements / with stocks
  223          MOVE  'PA_NDSTO'     TO  l_category.
  224        ENDIF.
  225      ELSE.
  226  *     material with movements
  227  *
  228        IF      bestand-anfmenge  IS INITIAL  AND
  229                bestand-/cwm/anfmenge  IS INITIAL  AND
  230                bestand-anfwert   IS INITIAL.
  231  *       stock and value on start date are zero
  232          IF   bestand-endmenge  IS INITIAL  AND
  233               bestand-/cwm/endmenge  IS INITIAL  AND
  234               bestand-endwert   IS INITIAL.
  235  *         stock and value on end date are zero, too
  236            MOVE  'PA_WDZER'     TO  l_category.
  237          ELSE.
  238  *         stock and value on end date <> zero
  239            MOVE  'PA_WDZEW'     TO  l_category.
  240          ENDIF.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
21.07.26 S2A      Include RM07MLBD_FORM_02                      Page    215
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

  241        ELSE.
  242  *       stock and value on start date <> zero
  243          IF     bestand-endmenge  IS INITIAL  AND
  244                 bestand-/cwm/endmenge  IS INITIAL  AND
  245                 bestand-endwert   IS INITIAL.
  246  *         stock and value on end date are zero
  247            MOVE  'PA_WDWIZ'   TO  l_category.
  248          ELSEIF bestand-endmenge = bestand-anfmenge  AND
  249                 bestand-/cwm/endmenge = bestand-/cwm/anfmenge  AND
  250                 bestand-anfwert  = bestand-endwert.
  251  *         stock and value on end date are equal
  252            MOVE  'PA_WDWEW'   TO  l_category.
  253          ELSE.
  254  *         stock and values on end date are differnt
  255            MOVE  'PA_WDWUW'   TO  l_category.
  256          ENDIF.
  257        ENDIF.
  258      ENDIF.
  259  ENHANCEMENT-POINT ehp605_rm07mlbd_form_02_01 SPOTS es_rm07mlbd .
  260

  264                                                              "n599218
  265      IF  sy-subrc IS INITIAL.                                "n599218
  266        IF  <l_fs> IS INITIAL.                                "n599218
  267          DELETE               bestand.                       "n599218
  268        ENDIF.                                                "n599218
  269      ENDIF.                                                  "n599218
  270    ENDLOOP.                                                  "n599218
  271  ENDFORM.                               " LISTUMFANG

  344  FORM f0000_create_table_g_t_organ
  345                     USING     l_f_error TYPE stype_organ-keytype.
  346
  347    DATA: l_ra_bukrs TYPE RANGE OF bukrs,                      "3116194
  348          l_bukrs    TYPE bukrs.                               "3116194
  349
  350  * at least on of these 3 range tables must be filled for the creation
  351  * of table g_t_organ
  352  * field  description         range table
  353  * -----  -----------         -----------
  354  * werks  plant               g_0000_ra_plant
  355  * bwkey  valuation area      g_0000_ra_bwkey
  356  * bukrs  company code        g_0000_ra_plant
  357
  358  * table g_t_organ must be empty
  359    CHECK : g_t_organ[] IS INITIAL.                           "n433765
  360
  361  * START OF CHANGE for note 1049935                         "n1049935
  362  * First check if there was a selection for company code    "n1049935
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
21.07.26 S2A      Include RM07MLBD_FORM_02                      Page    217
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

  363  * then do the F9000_AUTH_PLANT_CHECK only for necessary    "n1049935
  364  * selected items..                                         "n1049935
  365
  366  * select all plant from table t001w
  367    SELECT * FROM t001w        WHERE  werks  IN  g_0000_ra_werks.
  368
  369  *   check the valuation area
  370      CHECK : t001w-bwkey IN g_0000_ra_bwkey.
  371
  372  *   read the valuation area
  373      SELECT SINGLE * FROM t001k
  374                               WHERE  bwkey  =  t001w-bwkey.
  375
  376      CHECK : sy-subrc IS INITIAL.       "entry found ?
  377
  378  *   company code is required ?
  379      CHECK : t001k-bukrs IN g_0000_ra_bukrs.
  380
  381      SELECT SINGLE * FROM t001  WHERE  bukrs  =  t001k-bukrs.

  458
  459    DATA : l_f_type(01)        TYPE c.
  460
  461  * find out the fields of structure g_s_mseg_lean

  479        WHEN  OTHERS.

  520  *----------------------------------------------------------------------*

  522  *----------------------------------------------------------------------*
  523
  524  FORM f0600_create_range_lgort.
  525
  526    REFRESH                    g_ra_lgort.
  527    CLEAR                      g_ra_lgort.
  528
  529    IF      lgbst = 'X'.       "only Storage loc./batch stock
  530  *   copy the existing select-options
  531      MOVE lgort[]               TO  g_ra_lgort[].
  532
  533  *   add an exclusion for storage location = space
  534      MOVE : 'E'               TO  g_ra_lgort-sign,
  535             'EQ'              TO  g_ra_lgort-option.
  536      APPEND                   g_ra_lgort.
  537
  538    ELSEIF  bwbst = 'X'.       "only valuated stocks
  539  *   copy the existing select-options
  540      MOVE lgort[]               TO  g_ra_lgort[].
  541
  542    ELSEIF  sbbst = 'X'.       "only special stocks
  543      IF      sobkz  =  'O'  OR
  544              sobkz  =  'V'  OR
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
21.07.26 S2A      Include RM07MLBD_FORM_02                      Page    220
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

  545              sobkz  =  'W'.
  546        MOVE lgort[]               TO  g_ra_lgort[].
  547  **     only records with storage location = space allowed
  548  *      MOVE : 'I'             TO  g_ra_lgort-sign,
  549  *             'EQ'            TO  g_ra_lgort-option.
  550  *      APPEND                 g_ra_lgort.
  551      ELSE.
  552  *     Copy the existing select-options
  553        MOVE lgort[]             TO  g_ra_lgort[].
  554      ENDIF.
  555    ENDIF.
  556
  557  ENDFORM.                     "f0600_create_range_lgort

 1269  FORM f1100_check_lgort_sokzg.
 1270    CLEAR                      g_flag_delete.

 1272    IF  bwbst = 'X'.

 1407  FORM f9000_auth_plant_check
 1408                     USING     l_f_werks LIKE marc-werks.
 1409
 1410    CLEAR                      g_flag_authority.
 1411    ADD  1                     TO  g_f_cnt_before.
 1412
 1413    READ TABLE g_t_auth_plant  WITH KEY
 1414                               werks = l_f_werks BINARY SEARCH.
 1415
 1416    IF sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
 1417  *   plant found in buffer; take the result from the buffer
 1418      MOVE  g_t_auth_plant-ok            TO  g_flag_authority.
 1419    ELSE.
 1420  *   new plant / do the authority check / save result in buffer table
 1421      AUTHORITY-CHECK OBJECT 'M_MSEG_WMB'
 1422                      ID 'ACTVT' FIELD actvt03
 1423                      ID 'WERKS' FIELD  l_f_werks.
 1424
 1425      IF  sy-subrc IS INITIAL.
 1426        MOVE : 'X'             TO  g_t_auth_plant-ok,
 1427               'X'             TO  g_flag_authority.
 1428      ELSE.
 1429        CLEAR : g_t_auth_plant-ok, g_flag_authority.
 1430      ENDIF.
 1431
 1432      MOVE  l_f_werks          TO  g_t_auth_plant-werks.
 1433      APPEND                   g_t_auth_plant.
 1434      SORT                     g_t_auth_plant.
 1435    ENDIF.
 1436
 1437    IF  g_flag_authority = 'X'.
 1438      ADD  1                   TO  g_f_cnt_after.
 1439    ENDIF.
 1440
 1441  ENDFORM.                     "f9000_authority_check_plant
